<p><b>Kylian Mbappé Lottin</b> (born 20 December 1998) is a French professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)" title="Forward (association football)">forward</a> for <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> club <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> and the <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France national team</a>. Widely considered as one of the best players in the world, he is known for his <a href="/wiki/Dribbling" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a>, explosive speed, and clinical finishing.
</p><p>Mbappé began his senior career with Ligue 1 club <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a>, making his professional debut in 2015, aged 16. With them, he won a Ligue 1 title, <a href="/wiki/Troph%C3%A9es_UNFP_du_football#Young_Player_of_the_Year" title="Trophées UNFP du football">Ligue 1 Young Player of the Year</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Golden_Boy_(award)" title="Golden Boy (award)">Golden Boy</a> award. In 2017, he signed for league rivals Paris Saint-Germain on an initial loan, which was made permanent in 2018 in a <a href="/wiki/Transfer_(association_football)" title="Transfer (association football)">transfer</a> worth €180&#160;million, making him both the second-<a href="/wiki/List_of_most_expensive_association_football_transfers" title="List of most expensive association football transfers">most expensive player</a> and most expensive teenager.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> There, Mbappé won three Ligue 1 titles, two <a href="/wiki/Coupe_de_France" title="Coupe de France">Coupe de France</a> titles, was named <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1_Player_of_the_Year" title="Ligue 1 Player of the Year">Ligue 1 Player of the Year</a>, and has finished as <a href="/wiki/List_of_Ligue_1_top_scorers" title="List of Ligue 1 top scorers">Ligue 1 top scorer</a> twice. He is also the <a href="/wiki/List_of_Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C._records_and_statistics#All-time_top_scorers" title="List of Paris Saint-Germain F.C. records and statistics">third-highest goalscorer in the club's history</a>.
</p><p>At international level, Mbappé made his senior debut for France in 2017, at age 18. At the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>, Mbappé became the youngest French player to score at a World Cup, and became the second teenager, after <a href="/wiki/Pel%C3%A9" title="Pelé">Pelé</a>, to score in a <a href="/wiki/List_of_FIFA_World_Cup_finals" title="List of FIFA World Cup finals">World Cup Final</a>. He finished as the joint second-highest goalscorer as France won the tournament, and he received the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup_awards#Best_Young_Player_Award" title="FIFA World Cup awards">Best Young Player</a> and <a href="/wiki/French_Player_of_the_Year" title="French Player of the Year">French Player of the Year</a> awards for his performances.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life">Early life</span></h2>
<p>Mbappé was born in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> and was raised in <a href="/wiki/Bondy" title="Bondy">Bondy</a>, Seine-Saint-Denis, a commune 10.9&#160;km (6.8&#160;mi) from the centre of Paris.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> His father, Wilfried, is from Cameroon, and, as well as being Mbappé's agent, is a football coach, while his mother, Fayza Lamari, is of Algerian (<a href="/wiki/Kabyle_people" title="Kabyle people">Kabyle</a>) origin and is a former <a href="/wiki/Handball" title="Handball">handball</a> player.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Youth_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Youth-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> He has a younger brother, Ethan, who played for PSG's under-12 squad in 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Mbappé's adoptive brother, <a href="/wiki/Jir%C3%A8s_Kembo_Ekoko" title="Jirès Kembo Ekoko">Jirès Kembo Ekoko</a>, is also a professional football player.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Growing up, his idol was <a href="/wiki/Cristiano_Ronaldo" title="Cristiano Ronaldo">Cristiano Ronaldo</a>, a player he looked to emulate.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_career">Early career</span></h3>
<div class="quotebox pullquote floatright" style="width:28%; ;"><style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1012376600">.mw-parser-output .quotebox{background-color:#F9F9F9;border:1px solid #aaa;box-sizing:border-box;padding:10px;font-size:88%;max-width:100%}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft{margin:0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright{margin:0.5em 0 0.8em 1.4em}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.centered{margin:0.5em auto 0.8em auto}.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatleft p,.mw-parser-output .quotebox.floatright p{font-style:inherit}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-title{background-color:#F9F9F9;text-align:center;font-size:larger;font-weight:bold}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:before{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" “ ";vertical-align:-45%;line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox-quote.quoted:after{font-family:"Times New Roman",serif;font-weight:bold;font-size:large;color:gray;content:" ” ";line-height:0}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .left-aligned{text-align:left}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .right-aligned{text-align:right}.mw-parser-output .quotebox .center-aligned{text-align:center}.mw-parser-output .quotebox cite{display:block;font-style:normal}@media screen and (max-width:640px){.mw-parser-output .quotebox{width:100%!important;margin:0 0 0.8em!important;float:none!important}}</style>
<div class="quotebox-quote left-aligned" style="">"He had technique and vision in the game that most children just don't have. He's got eyes in the back of his head. He knows how to anticipate where the ball will go. Here, he never played for his proper age group, he always played with older children because there was no point leaving him with kids his own age."</div>
<p><cite class="left-aligned" style="">—Atmane Airouche, president of AS Bondy, on Mbappé as a child.<sup id="cite_ref-Youth_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Youth-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup></cite>
</p>
</div>
<p>Mbappé began his career at AS Bondy, coached by his father, Wilfried. Another of his youth coaches at AS Bondy, Antonio Riccardi, stated,
</p>
<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r996844942">.mw-parser-output .templatequote{overflow:hidden;margin:1em 0;padding:0 40px}.mw-parser-output .templatequote .templatequotecite{line-height:1.5em;text-align:left;padding-left:1.6em;margin-top:0}</style><blockquote class="templatequote"><p>The first time I coached him was when he was six years old. You could tell he was different. Kylian could do much more than the other children. His dribbling was already fantastic and he was much faster than the others. He was the best player I've ever seen in 15 years coaching here. In Paris, there are many talents but I'd never seen a talent like him. He was what we call a 'crack' (the best).<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup></p></blockquote>
<p>Eventually, he moved to the <a href="/wiki/INF_Clairefontaine" title="INF Clairefontaine">Clairefontaine</a> academy, putting on a host of impressive performances leading to numerous French clubs, and <a href="/wiki/Real_Madrid_CF" title="Real Madrid CF">Real Madrid</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a>, <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a>, <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a> and <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a>, attempting to sign him.<sup id="cite_ref-Youth_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Youth-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> At the age of 11, Real Madrid invited Mbappé to train with their under-12s and visit the club's facilities.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> At age 14 he travelled to London after an invite from Chelsea, playing a match for their youth team against <a href="/wiki/Charlton_Athletic_F.C." title="Charlton Athletic F.C.">Charlton Athletic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> He ultimately settled on <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-youthcareer_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-youthcareer-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Monaco">Monaco</span></h3>
<h4><span id="2015.E2.80.9316:_Development"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–16:_Development">2015–16: Development</span></h4>
<p>Mbappé made his first team debut on 2 December 2015 in a 1–1 <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> home draw against <a href="/wiki/Stade_Malherbe_Caen" title="Stade Malherbe Caen">SM Caen</a>, replacing <a href="/wiki/F%C3%A1bio_Coentr%C3%A3o" title="Fábio Coentrão">Fábio Coentrão</a> after 88 minutes. He therefore became Monaco's youngest-ever first-team player aged 16 years and 347 days, breaking <a href="/wiki/Thierry_Henry" title="Thierry Henry">Thierry Henry</a>'s record set 21 years previously.<sup id="cite_ref-youthcareer_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-youthcareer-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-soccerway_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soccerway-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 20 February 2016, Mbappé scored his first goal for the club's first team, a stoppage-time goal in a home Ligue 1 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Troyes_AC" title="Troyes AC">Troyes</a>; at the age of 17 years and 62 days, he became the youngest first team goalscorer in Monaco's history—once again displacing Henry in the process.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> On 6 March 2016, Mbappé signed his first professional contract, a three-year deal, tying him to Monaco until June 2019.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> In an interview with <a href="/wiki/CNN" title="CNN">CNN</a>, <a href="/wiki/Vadim_Vasilyev_(businessman)" title="Vadim Vasilyev (businessman)">Vadim Vasilyev</a>, AS Monaco's vice-president, who played a key role in Mbappé signing his first professional contract with the Ligue 1 club, stated that he knew early on that Mbappé was a "phenomenon."<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317:_Breakthrough_and_league_title"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–17:_Breakthrough_and_league_title">2016–17: Breakthrough and league title</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Mbappe.PNG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c3/Mbappe.PNG/170px-Mbappe.PNG" decoding="async" width="170" height="368" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/c/c3/Mbappe.PNG 1.5x" data-file-width="195" data-file-height="422" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Mbappe.PNG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mbappé warming up for <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a> in 2017</div></div></div>
<p>Mbappé scored the first <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick_(association_football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Hat-trick (association football)">hat-trick</a> of his first team career on 14 December 2016 in the 7–0 rout of <a href="/wiki/Stade_Rennais_F.C." title="Stade Rennais F.C.">Stade Rennais</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Coupe_de_la_Ligue" title="2016–17 Coupe de la Ligue">Coupe de la Ligue</a> round of 16 at the <a href="/wiki/Stade_Louis_II" title="Stade Louis II">Stade Louis II</a><sup id="cite_ref-soccerway_18-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soccerway-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> – the first hat-trick scored by any Monaco player in the competition since <a href="/wiki/Sonny_Anderson" title="Sonny Anderson">Sonny Anderson</a> in 1997.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 11 February 2017, Mbappé scored the first Ligue 1 hat-trick of his career in the 5–0 home win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Metz" title="FC Metz">Metz</a>; at 18 years and two months he became the youngest player to score a Ligue 1 hat-trick since <a href="/wiki/J%C3%A9r%C3%A9my_M%C3%A9nez" title="Jérémy Ménez">Jérémy Ménez</a> did it for <a href="/wiki/FC_Sochaux-Montb%C3%A9liard" title="FC Sochaux-Montbéliard">FC Sochaux-Montbéliard</a> back in 2005.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 21 February, Mbappé scored Monaco's second goal in the 40th minute with a half-volley after receiving <a href="/wiki/Fabinho_(footballer,_born_1993)" title="Fabinho (footballer, born 1993)">Fabinho</a>'s long ball over the opponents' back line (it was his first ever <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Europa_League" title="UEFA Europa League">UEFA Europa League</a> or <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">UEFA Champions League</a> goal and he became the second youngest French scorer in UEFA Champions League history behind <a href="/wiki/Karim_Benzema" title="Karim Benzema">Karim Benzema</a>) in the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase" title="2016–17 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">UEFA Champions League round of 16 first leg match</a> against Manchester City, which Monaco lost 5–3.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> On 5 March, Mbappé scored two first-half goals in the 4–0 Ligue 1 home win over <a href="/wiki/FC_Nantes" title="FC Nantes">Nantes</a> to bring his Ligue 1 career tally to ten goals and become the youngest player in the last 30 years to hit the <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a>/Division 1 ten-career-goals mark. His brace against Nantes on 5 March brought up his <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_AS_Monaco_FC_season" title="2016–17 AS Monaco FC season">2016–17 season</a> tally to nine Ligue 1 goals and five Ligue 1 assists in just 822 minutes of Ligue 1 football.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> On 11 March, he scored a goal in the 2–1 Ligue 1 home win against <a href="/wiki/FC_Girondins_de_Bordeaux" title="FC Girondins de Bordeaux">FC Girondins de Bordeaux</a> to register his seventh Ligue 1 goal in his last four starts.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the UEFA Champions League round of 16-second leg match at the Stade Louis II on 15 March, he made the score 1–0 for Monaco in the 8th minute by turning home <a href="/wiki/Bernardo_Silva" title="Bernardo Silva">Bernardo Silva</a>'s low cross from close-range (his 11th goal in his past 11 matches in all competitions) to help Monaco beat Manchester City 3–1 (aggregate score 6–6) and advance to the quarter-finals on the <a href="/wiki/Away_goals_rule" title="Away goals rule">away goals rule</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> In the quarter-finals against <a href="/wiki/Borussia_Dortmund" title="Borussia Dortmund">Borussia Dortmund</a>, Mbappé won a penalty and scored two goals as Monaco won the away leg 3–2.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> In the second leg, Mbappé opened the scoring as Monaco won 3–1 and advanced to the semi-finals.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Monaco were eliminated from the Champions League 4–1 on aggregate by <a href="/wiki/Juventus_F.C." title="Juventus F.C.">Juventus</a>, with Mbappé scoring Monaco's lone goal in the second leg.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> Mbappé ended the <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_Ligue_1" title="2016–17 Ligue 1">2016–17 season</a> with 26 goals from 44 matches in all competitions as Monaco won the Ligue 1 title.<sup id="cite_ref-loan_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-loan-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Paris_Saint-Germain">Paris Saint-Germain</span></h3>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9318:_World_record_transfer_and_treble"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–18:_World_record_transfer_and_treble">2017–18: World record transfer and treble</span></h4>
<p>On 31 August 2017, <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> announced the signing of Mbappé from Monaco on <a href="/wiki/Loan_(sports)" title="Loan (sports)">loan</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> The fee required for a subsequent full transfer was set at a rumoured €145&#160;million plus €35&#160;million in add-ons, making him the most expensive teenager ever, the most expensive transfer ever within a domestic league, and potentially the <a href="/wiki/List_of_most_expensive_association_football_transfers" title="List of most expensive association football transfers">second most expensive player</a> ever, behind teammate <a href="/wiki/Neymar" title="Neymar">Neymar</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> He was handed the number 29 shirt upon arrival in the French capital.<sup id="cite_ref-PSG_number_41-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PSG_number-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He scored on his debut on 8 September in a 5–1 Ligue 1 win at Metz, in which <a href="/wiki/Beno%C3%AEt_Assou-Ekotto" title="Benoît Assou-Ekotto">Benoît Assou-Ekotto</a> was <a href="/wiki/Ejection_(sports)" title="Ejection (sports)">sent off</a> for fouling him.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Four days later, Mbappé recorded his first European goal for <i>Les Parisiens</i> in a 5–0 <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League group stage">UEFA Champions League group stage</a> away defeat of <a href="/wiki/Celtic_F.C." title="Celtic F.C.">Celtic</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> He starred in PSG's 3–0 victory over Bayern Munich in the second group game of the Champions League, setting up goals for <a href="/wiki/Edinson_Cavani" title="Edinson Cavani">Edinson Cavani</a> and Neymar, the latter seeing him taking out a defender with a <a href="/wiki/Dummy_(football)" title="Dummy (football)">feint</a> by rolling the ball under his foot.<sup id="cite_ref-LES_44-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LES-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> On 6 December, Mbappé scored his 10th Champions League goal in a 3–1 defeat to Bayern Munich and became the youngest player to reach that mark at the age of 18 years and 11 months.<sup id="cite_ref-CL_record_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CL_record-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> Having won his first league title with the club, on 8 May 2018, Mbappé played as PSG won 2–0 against <a href="/wiki/Les_Herbiers_VF" title="Les Herbiers VF">Les Herbiers VF</a> to clinch the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_Coupe_de_France" title="2017–18 Coupe de France">2017–18 Coupe de France</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2018.E2.80.9319:_Ligue_1_Player_of_the_Year"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2018–19:_Ligue_1_Player_of_the_Year">2018–19: Ligue 1 Player of the Year</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93088.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93088.jpg/170px-2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93088.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="211" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93088.jpg/255px-2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93088.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a2/2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93088.jpg/340px-2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93088.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2973" data-file-height="3695" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93088.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mbappé with <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">Paris Saint-Germain</a> in 2019</div></div></div>
<p>In July 2018, Mbappé was given the number 7 jersey for the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C._season" title="2018–19 Paris Saint-Germain F.C. season">upcoming season</a> with PSG, taking up the squad number vacated by <a href="/wiki/Lucas_Moura" title="Lucas Moura">Lucas Moura</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-number_7_47-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-number_7-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Sporting the hashtag #K7LIAN, Mbappé stated, "I keep trying to progress on the pitch and I think that, for me, it was the right time to change number. It is something of an affirmation. The No. 7 shirt is a legendary one and many greats have worn it. I hope that I will be able to do this number justice on the pitch."<sup id="cite_ref-number_7_47-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-number_7-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In his first appearance of the season, Mbappé scored twice in the last 10 minutes as PSG won 3–1 against <a href="/wiki/En_Avant_de_Guingamp" class="mw-redirect" title="En Avant de Guingamp">Guingamp</a> in Ligue 1.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> In the following league game, the front three of Mbappé, Cavani and Neymar all scored in a 3–1 win over <a href="/wiki/Angers_SCO" title="Angers SCO">Angers</a> at home, with Mbappé – starting his first game of the season – scoring from a volley and setting up Neymar to score the third.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> On 1 September, he scored and assisted in a 4–2 away win over <a href="/wiki/N%C3%AEmes_Olympique" title="Nîmes Olympique">Nîmes</a>, but was <a href="/wiki/Ejection_(sports)#Association_football" title="Ejection (sports)">sent off</a> for the first time in his career with a straight red card in injury time, after shoving <a href="/wiki/T%C3%A9ji_Savanier" title="Téji Savanier">Téji Savanier</a> in retaliation for a late challenge from behind, for which Savanier was also sent off.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Regarding his sending-off, Mbappé told reporters after the match, "If I had the chance to do it over again, I would do the same thing. I will apologise to the supporters and everybody, but I cannot tolerate this sort of thing."<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> On 8 October, Mbappé scored four goals in just 13 minutes in a 5–0 home victory over <a href="/wiki/Olympique_Lyonnais" title="Olympique Lyonnais">Lyon</a> and became the youngest player (19 years and 9 months) to score four goals in one game in Ligue 1 over the last 45 seasons.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On 3 December, Mbappé was the inaugural winner of the <a href="/wiki/Kopa_Trophy" title="Kopa Trophy">Kopa Trophy</a>, which is awarded by <i><a href="/wiki/France_Football" title="France Football">France Football</a></i> to the best player in the world under the age of 21.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 19 January 2019, Mbappé was one of two players (the other being Cavani) to score a hat-trick in a 9–0 win over Guingamp, breaking a record PSG set the previous season.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> On 12 February, he scored a goal in a 2–0 win over <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a> at <a href="/wiki/Old_Trafford" title="Old Trafford">Old Trafford</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2018–19 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> round of 16.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> On 2 March, he scored twice in a 2–1 away win over Caen to reach his 50th goal with the club.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> On 21 April, he scored a hat-trick in a 3–1 win against Monaco, to be his first goals against his former club.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> PSG finished the season as Ligue 1 champions,<sup id="cite_ref-ligue1history_58-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ligue1history-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> with Mbappé winning the <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1_Player_of_the_Year" title="Ligue 1 Player of the Year">Player of the Year</a> award,<sup id="cite_ref-UNFP_59-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-UNFP-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> while also finishing the season as the <a href="/wiki/2018%E2%80%9319_Ligue_1#Top_goalscorers" title="2018–19 Ligue 1">top goalscorer</a> with 33 goals.<sup id="cite_ref-ligue1history_58-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-ligue1history-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320:_Back-to-back_league_top_goalscorer"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20:_Back-to-back_league_top_goalscorer">2019–20: Back-to-back league top goalscorer</span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93616.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93616.jpg/220px-2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93616.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="240" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93616.jpg/330px-2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93616.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/ad/2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93616.jpg/440px-2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93616.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2242" data-file-height="2449" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:2019-07-17_SG_Dynamo_Dresden_vs._Paris_Saint-Germain_by_Sandro_Halank%E2%80%93616.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mbappé playing against Dynamo Dresden in July 2019</div></div></div>
<p>On 3 August, Mbappé scored in a 2–1 win over Rennes to capture his first title of the 2019–20 season, the <a href="/wiki/2019_Troph%C3%A9e_des_Champions" title="2019 Trophée des Champions">2019 Trophée des Champions</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-2019TDC_60-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2019TDC-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> He then scored again in PSG's opening <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_Ligue_1" title="2019–20 Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a> match of the season, a 3–0 home win over Nîmes on 11 August.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> On 22 October, he came off the bench and scored a <a href="/wiki/Perfect_hat-trick" class="mw-redirect" title="Perfect hat-trick">perfect hat-trick</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> in a 5–0 away win over Belgian side <a href="/wiki/Club_Brugge_KV" title="Club Brugge KV">Club Brugge</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2019%E2%80%9320_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2019–20 UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a>; at the age of 20 years and 306 days, he became the youngest player ever to score at least 15 goals in the competition.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 1 May 2020, PSG were crowned Ligue 1 champions after the season had been called off amid the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic_in_France" title="COVID-19 pandemic in France">COVID-19 pandemic</a>; at the time of the League's premature suspension, PSG were in first place, with a twelve–point lead over second–placed <a href="/wiki/Olympique_de_Marseille" title="Olympique de Marseille">Marseille</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup> Mbappé finished the 2019–20 season as joint-top scorer in Ligue 1 with 18 goals, along with <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Wissam_Ben_Yedder" title="Wissam Ben Yedder">Wissam Ben Yedder</a>. However, Mbappé was assigned the title of top scorer due to his superior goals per game ratio.<sup id="cite_ref-2019–20_Ligue_1_top_scorer_66-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2019–20_Ligue_1_top_scorer-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> On 24 July, in the <a href="/wiki/2020_Coupe_de_France_Final" title="2020 Coupe de France Final">2020 Coupe de France Final</a> against <a href="/wiki/AS_Saint-%C3%89tienne" title="AS Saint-Étienne">Saint-Étienne</a>, Mbappé was forced off after sustaining an injury following a challenge from <a href="/wiki/Lo%C3%AFc_Perrin" title="Loïc Perrin">Loïc Perrin</a>, who was sent off; PSG won the match 1–0,<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> although Mbappé was ruled out of the <a href="/wiki/2020_Coupe_de_la_Ligue_Final" title="2020 Coupe de la Ligue Final">2020 Coupe de la Ligue Final</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup> which PSG went on to win, completing a domestic treble.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> He returned to action in the Champions League quarter-final against <a href="/wiki/Atalanta_B.C." title="Atalanta B.C.">Atalanta</a> on 12 August, coming on a substitute, and assisting <a href="/wiki/Eric_Maxim_Choupo-Moting" title="Eric Maxim Choupo-Moting">Choupo-Moting</a>'s match–winning goal in injury time.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> PSG eventually lost out in the <a href="/wiki/2020_UEFA_Champions_League_Final" title="2020 UEFA Champions League Final">Champions League final</a> 1–0 to <a href="/wiki/FC_Bayern_Munich" title="FC Bayern Munich">Bayern Munich</a> on 23 August.<sup id="cite_ref-CL_2020_71-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CL_2020-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321:_COVID-19_and_goalscoring_achievements"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21:_COVID-19_and_goalscoring_achievements">2020–21: COVID-19 and goalscoring achievements</span></h4>
<p>Mbappé missed the first three matches of the season after contracting the <a href="/wiki/Coronavirus_disease_2019" class="mw-redirect" title="Coronavirus disease 2019">coronavirus</a> while playing with the France national team.<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> He returned to action on 20 September 2020 in a 3–0 away win against <a href="/wiki/OGC_Nice" title="OGC Nice">Nice</a>, and scored a goal from a penalty kick.<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup> On 28 October, Mbappé recorded two assists, both for <a href="/wiki/Moise_Kean" title="Moise Kean">Moise Kean</a>, in a 2–0 <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Champions_League_group_stage" title="2020–21 UEFA Champions League group stage">Champions League group stage</a> victory against <a href="/wiki/%C4%B0stanbul_Ba%C5%9Fak%C5%9Fehir_F.K." title="stanbul Baakehir F.K.">stanbul Baakehir</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> In doing so, he became the player with the most assists in the competition since the beginning of the <a href="/wiki/2017%E2%80%9318_UEFA_Champions_League" title="2017–18 UEFA Champions League">2017–18 edition</a>, with his tally adding up to fourteen over the four seasons.<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup> In a Ligue 1 match against <a href="/wiki/Montpellier_HSC" title="Montpellier HSC">Montpellier</a> on 5 December, Mbappé scored his 100th goal for PSG, becoming only the fifth player to achieve the feat for the Parisian club.<sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> In his side's final Champions League group match, Mbappé scored his first two goals of the European campaign against Baakehir, as PSG won 5–1 and qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2020%E2%80%9321_UEFA_Champions_League_knockout_phase" title="2020–21 UEFA Champions League knockout phase">knockout phase</a> as group winners.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> He also became the youngest player in Champions League history to reach twenty goals (although this record would then be surpassed later on in the same season by <a href="/wiki/Erling_Haaland" title="Erling Haaland">Erling Haaland</a>).<sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 16 February 2021, Mbappé became only the third player, after <a href="/wiki/Faustino_Asprilla" title="Faustino Asprilla">Faustino Asprilla</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andriy_Shevchenko" title="Andriy Shevchenko">Andriy Shevchenko</a>, to score a <a href="/wiki/List_of_UEFA_Champions_League_hat-tricks" title="List of UEFA Champions League hat-tricks">Champions League hat-trick</a> against <a href="/wiki/FC_Barcelona" title="FC Barcelona">Barcelona</a>, doing so in PSG's 4–1 round of 16 win at the <a href="/wiki/Camp_Nou" title="Camp Nou">Camp Nou</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> Mbappé's hat-trick also saw him overtake <a href="/wiki/Pauleta" title="Pauleta">Pauleta</a>'s total of 109 goals to become PSG's <a href="/wiki/List_of_Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C._records_and_statistics#All-time_top_scorers" title="List of Paris Saint-Germain F.C. records and statistics">third-highest scorer</a>, with only Cavani (200 goals) and <a href="/wiki/Zlatan_Ibrahimovi%C4%87" title="Zlatan Ibrahimovi">Zlatan Ibrahimovi</a> (156 goals) getting more for the club.<sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> On 27 February, Mbappé scored twice in a 4–0 away win against <a href="/wiki/Dijon_FCO" title="Dijon FCO">Dijon</a>, becoming the first player to score five braces in the Ligue 1 season.<sup id="cite_ref-82" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> In the second leg against Barcelona on 10 March, Mbappé scored from the spot in a 1–1 draw at the Parc de Princes, as his side advanced to the quarter-finals 5–2 on aggregate.<sup id="cite_ref-83" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> Mbappé's penalty was his 25th Champions League goal, surpassing opponent <a href="/wiki/Lionel_Messi" title="Lionel Messi">Lionel Messi</a> as the youngest player to reach this milestone, aged 22 years and 80 days. Adding to his hat-trick from the first leg, Mbappé additionally became the first player to score four goals against Barcelona in a single Champions League season.<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Youth_career_and_early_senior_career">Youth career and early senior career</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kylian_Mbappe_celebrating_-_March_2018_(cropped).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Kylian_Mbappe_celebrating_-_March_2018_%28cropped%29.jpg/170px-Kylian_Mbappe_celebrating_-_March_2018_%28cropped%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="227" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Kylian_Mbappe_celebrating_-_March_2018_%28cropped%29.jpg/255px-Kylian_Mbappe_celebrating_-_March_2018_%28cropped%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6e/Kylian_Mbappe_celebrating_-_March_2018_%28cropped%29.jpg/340px-Kylian_Mbappe_celebrating_-_March_2018_%28cropped%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="469" data-file-height="627" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kylian_Mbappe_celebrating_-_March_2018_(cropped).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mbappé playing for <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a> in March 2018</div></div></div>
<p>Mbappé capped a fine debut senior season at Monaco by scoring five times for <a href="/wiki/France_national_under-19_football_team" title="France national under-19 football team">France</a> as they won the <a href="/wiki/2016_UEFA_European_Under-19_Championship" title="2016 UEFA European Under-19 Championship">2016 UEFA European Under-19 Championship</a>, the striker almost single-handedly securing their spot in the final with a sparkling performance in their 3–1 victory against <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_under-19_football_team" title="Portugal national under-19 football team">Portugal</a> in the semi-finals.<sup id="cite_ref-youthcareer_17-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-youthcareer-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Mbappé was called up to the senior <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a> squad for the first time to face <a href="/wiki/Luxembourg_national_football_team" title="Luxembourg national football team">Luxembourg</a> and <a href="/wiki/Spain_national_football_team" title="Spain national football team">Spain</a> in March 2017.<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut on 25 March against the former side, coming on for <a href="/wiki/Dimitri_Payet" title="Dimitri Payet">Dimitri Payet</a> in the 78th minute of a 3–1 <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(UEFA)" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification (UEFA)">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification</a> away win.<sup id="cite_ref-soccerway_18-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soccerway-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> In doing so, he became the second youngest player ever (only behind <a href="/wiki/Maryan_Wisniewski" title="Maryan Wisniewski">Maryan Wisniewski</a>) to feature for France at 18 years, three months and five days old.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> On 31 August 2017, Mbappé scored his first senior international goal in a <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_UEFA_Group_A" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – UEFA Group A">2018 World Cup qualification</a> match against the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup> He scored twice against Russia in a friendly in March 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="2018_FIFA_World_Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</span></h3>
<p>On 17 May 2018, Mbappé was called up to the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_squads#France" title="2018 FIFA World Cup squads">France squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 World Cup</a> in Russia.<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> On 21 June 2018, he scored his first World Cup goal in France's 1–0 <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_Group_C" title="2018 FIFA World Cup Group C">Group C</a> win over <a href="/wiki/Peru_national_football_team" title="Peru national football team">Peru</a>. This made him the youngest French goalscorer in World Cup history at age 19.<sup id="cite_ref-fraper_90-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-fraper-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> On 30 June 2018, he was named <a href="/wiki/Player_of_the_match" title="Player of the match">man of the match</a> in a <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_knockout_stage#France_vs_Argentina" title="2018 FIFA World Cup knockout stage">4–3 win</a> over <a href="/wiki/Argentina_national_football_team" title="Argentina national football team">Argentina</a>, scoring twice and suffering a foul in the box which resulted in <a href="/wiki/Antoine_Griezmann" title="Antoine Griezmann">Antoine Griezmann</a> opening the score from a penalty kick.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> Mbappé was the second teenager to score two goals in a World Cup match after <a href="/wiki/Pel%C3%A9" title="Pelé">Pelé</a> in <a href="/wiki/1958_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1958 FIFA World Cup">1958</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup> In a post-match press conference, Mbappé stated: "It's flattering to be the second one after Pelé but let's put things into context – Pelé is in another category."<sup id="cite_ref-Pelé_1958_93-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pelé_1958-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 15 July, Mbappé scored with a 25-yard strike against <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_Final" title="2018 FIFA World Cup Final">2018 World Cup Final</a>, with France winning 4–2.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> He became the second teenager, after Pelé, to <a href="/wiki/List_of_FIFA_World_Cup_finals_goalscorers" class="mw-redirect" title="List of FIFA World Cup finals goalscorers">score in a World Cup Final</a>, and with four goals in the tournament he received the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup_awards#Best_Young_Player_Award" title="FIFA World Cup awards">FIFA World Cup Best Young Player Award</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> Pelé congratulated him on social media, and stated "welcome to the club".<sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Euro_2020_qualifying_and_2020.E2.80.9321_UEFA_Nations_League"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Euro_2020_qualifying_and_2020–21_UEFA_Nations_League">Euro 2020 qualifying and 2020–21 UEFA Nations League</span></h3>
<p>On 11 June 2019, Mbappé scored his 100th career goal in a 4–0 away win over <a href="/wiki/Andorra_national_football_team" title="Andorra national football team">Andorra</a> in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2020_qualifying" title="UEFA Euro 2020 qualifying">Euro 2020 qualifying</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 5 September 2020, Mbappé scored the only goal for France in a 1–0 <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Nations_League" title="UEFA Nations League">UEFA Nations League</a> win against <a href="/wiki/Sweden_national_football_team" title="Sweden national football team">Sweden</a>. However, two days after the game, he tested positive for <a href="/wiki/Coronavirus_disease_2019" class="mw-redirect" title="Coronavirus disease 2019">COVID-19</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> He made his return to play for France in a 7–1 victory against <a href="/wiki/Ukraine_national_football_team" title="Ukraine national football team">Ukraine</a> on 7 October 2020, a match in which he scored a goal and assisted another.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup> One week later, he scored the match-winning goal in a 2–1 win against <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Player_profile">Player profile</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play_and_reception">Style of play and reception</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kylian_Mbappe_2017.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Kylian_Mbappe_2017.jpg/170px-Kylian_Mbappe_2017.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="276" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Kylian_Mbappe_2017.jpg/255px-Kylian_Mbappe_2017.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/72/Kylian_Mbappe_2017.jpg/340px-Kylian_Mbappe_2017.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1188" data-file-height="1929" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kylian_Mbappe_2017.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mbappé's movement has been compared to former forwards <a href="/wiki/Thierry_Henry" title="Thierry Henry">Thierry Henry</a> and <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a></div></div></div>
<p>Mbappé has been described by <a href="/wiki/Ars%C3%A8ne_Wenger" title="Arsène Wenger">Arsène Wenger</a> as a "huge football talent" who "has similarities to Thierry Henry".<sup id="cite_ref-Arsene_103-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Arsene-103">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> His talent and precocious performances for France at the 2018 World Cup also led him to be compared to Pelé in the media.<sup id="cite_ref-104" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-104">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> A versatile forward, Mbappé often plays as a <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Winger" title="Forward (association football)">winger</a>, and is capable of playing on either flank, due to his ability with both feet.<sup id="cite_ref-better_than_Henry_105-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-better_than_Henry-105">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-106" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-106">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> He is capable of cutting into the centre onto his stronger right foot from the left wing, and is also capable of creating chances and providing assists for teammates from the right due to his vision.<sup id="cite_ref-wonderkid_107-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wonderkid-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-108" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-108">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-going_home_109-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-going_home-109">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-110" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-110">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup> He is also able to play in the <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Centre-forward" title="Forward (association football)">centre</a> as a main <a href="/wiki/Forward_(association_football)#Striker" title="Forward (association football)">striker</a>, due to his composure, clinical finishing, and eye for goal.<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Mbappe_at_19_113-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Mbappe_at_19-113">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-promessa_114-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-promessa-114">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> A highly skilful player, Mbappé is also known for his excellent <a href="/wiki/Dribbling#Association_football" title="Dribbling">dribbling</a> ability, as well as his explosive acceleration, agility, quick feet, and creativity when in possession of the ball, as demonstrated by his use of elaborate feints, such as <a href="/wiki/Step_over" title="Step over">step overs</a>, or sudden changes of pace or direction to beat opponents in one on one situations.<sup id="cite_ref-swapping_115-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-swapping-115">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-world_at_his_feet_116-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-world_at_his_feet-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> In spite of his tall lean frame, he is also an athletic player, gifted with physical strength.<sup id="cite_ref-118" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-118">&#91;118&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In addition to his technical skills, Mbappé is also highly regarded for his outstanding pace and close ball control when dribbling at speed, as well as his excellent movement, tactical intelligence, and ability to beat the defensive line by making attacking runs into space both on and off the ball.<sup id="cite_ref-wonderkid_107-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wonderkid-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-world_at_his_feet_116-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-world_at_his_feet-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup> His ability to time his runs enables him to stretch opposing defences, and also make him a dangerous offensive threat on counter-attacks.<sup id="cite_ref-wonderkid_107-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wonderkid-107">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-world_at_his_feet_116-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-world_at_his_feet-116">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-platform_119-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-platform-119">&#91;119&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-120" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-120">&#91;120&#93;</a></sup> In April 2017, former France international <a href="/wiki/Nicolas_Anelka" title="Nicolas Anelka">Nicolas Anelka</a> said that Mbappé's ability to run at defences reminded him of <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Football_at_the_1996_Summer_Olympics_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_tournament" title="Football at the 1996 Summer Olympics – Men&#39;s tournament">1996 Olympics</a> and that Mbappé had the characteristics of a world-class player.<sup id="cite_ref-121" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-121">&#91;121&#93;</a></sup> Mbappé was named the fastest player in the world in a ranking by French newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/Le_Figaro" title="Le Figaro">Le Figaro</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-122" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup> When <a href="/wiki/Stefan_de_Vrij" title="Stefan de Vrij">Stefan de Vrij</a>, central defender for <a href="/wiki/Inter_Milan" title="Inter Milan">Inter Milan</a> and the Netherlands, was asked of his toughest opponent, he placed Mbappé ahead of anyone else, including Mbappé's childhood idol Cristiano Ronaldo.<sup id="cite_ref-123" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-123">&#91;123&#93;</a></sup> In 2018, Mbappé was considered the world's most expensive player from a transfer value perspective by the <a href="/wiki/International_Centre_for_Sports_Studies" title="International Centre for Sports Studies">CIES</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-124" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-124">&#91;124&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Outside_football">Outside football</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span></h3>
<p>In a 2018 interview with <i><a href="/wiki/Time_(magazine)" title="Time (magazine)">Time</a></i>, Mbappé spoke about the sacrifices he made as a teenager to focus on his football development: "I did not have the moments of so-called normal people during adolescence, like going out with friends, enjoying good times." But despite missing out on a "normal" life, Mbappé states he is "living the life he always dreamed of".<sup id="cite_ref-Time_125-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Time-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> Just over four years after making his professional debut he has over 42 million <a href="/wiki/Instagram" title="Instagram">Instagram</a> followers.<sup id="cite_ref-Time_125-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Time-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup> While he admits his "life has been totally turned upside down" since he first entered the spotlight, he says he is "happy".<sup id="cite_ref-Time_125-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Time-125">&#91;125&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Media_and_sponsorship">Media and sponsorship</span></h3>
<p>Mbappé has a sponsorship deal with sportswear and equipment supplier <a href="/wiki/Nike,_Inc." title="Nike, Inc.">Nike</a>. In 2017, his prodigious talent saw Nike launch his own personalised football boots at age 18, the Kylian Mbappé <a href="/wiki/Nike_Hypervenom" title="Nike Hypervenom">Nike Hypervenom</a> 3.<sup id="cite_ref-126" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-126">&#91;126&#93;</a></sup> In 2018, he unveiled the <a href="/wiki/Nike_Mercurial_Vapor#Mercurial_Vapor_X_&amp;_Superfly_VI" title="Nike Mercurial Vapor">Nike Mercurial Superfly VI</a> boots which were inspired by the R9 Mercurial boots of former Brazilian striker Ronaldo.<sup id="cite_ref-127" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-127">&#91;127&#93;</a></sup> In 2018, Swiss watchmaker <a href="/wiki/Hublot" title="Hublot">Hublot</a> signed Mbappé as a global ambassador.<sup id="cite_ref-128" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-128">&#91;128&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Mbappé features in <a href="/wiki/EA_Sports" title="EA Sports">EA Sports</a>' <a href="/wiki/FIFA_(video_game_series)" title="FIFA (video game series)"><i>FIFA</i> video game series</a>:
on <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_18" title="FIFA 18">FIFA 18</a></i> he had the highest potential rating of 94.<sup id="cite_ref-129" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-129">&#91;129&#93;</a></sup> His trademark <a href="/wiki/Goal_celebration" title="Goal celebration">goal celebration</a> – posing with his arms folded and hands tucked under his armpits – was inspired by his younger brother Ethan who would celebrate in this manner when beating Kylian at <i>FIFA</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-130" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-130">&#91;130&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-131" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-131">&#91;131&#93;</a></sup> The celebration appears in <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_19" title="FIFA 19">FIFA 19</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-132" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-132">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup> Mbappé features as the cover star of <i><a href="/wiki/FIFA_21" title="FIFA 21">FIFA 21</a></i>, making him the youngest to appear on the cover solo.<sup id="cite_ref-133" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-133">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Philanthropy">Philanthropy</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kylian_Mbapp%C3%A9_receives_the_best_young_player_award_at_the_2018_Football_World_Cup_Russia.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Kylian_Mbapp%C3%A9_receives_the_best_young_player_award_at_the_2018_Football_World_Cup_Russia.jpg/220px-Kylian_Mbapp%C3%A9_receives_the_best_young_player_award_at_the_2018_Football_World_Cup_Russia.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="136" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Kylian_Mbapp%C3%A9_receives_the_best_young_player_award_at_the_2018_Football_World_Cup_Russia.jpg/330px-Kylian_Mbapp%C3%A9_receives_the_best_young_player_award_at_the_2018_Football_World_Cup_Russia.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Kylian_Mbapp%C3%A9_receives_the_best_young_player_award_at_the_2018_Football_World_Cup_Russia.jpg/440px-Kylian_Mbapp%C3%A9_receives_the_best_young_player_award_at_the_2018_Football_World_Cup_Russia.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1880" data-file-height="1160" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kylian_Mbapp%C3%A9_receives_the_best_young_player_award_at_the_2018_Football_World_Cup_Russia.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Mbappé (pictured receiving his FIFA World Cup young player award next to French president <a href="/wiki/Emmanuel_Macron" title="Emmanuel Macron">Emmanuel Macron</a>) met with the president in February 2018 to discuss a sports project in Africa</div></div></div>
<p>On 22 February 2018, Mbappé was joined by two of Africa's greatest strikers, former <a href="/wiki/A.C._Milan" title="A.C. Milan">A.C. Milan</a> forward and current Liberia President <a href="/wiki/George_Weah" title="George Weah">George Weah</a>, and former Chelsea and Ivory Coast forward <a href="/wiki/Didier_Drogba" title="Didier Drogba">Didier Drogba</a>, in a meeting with French President <a href="/wiki/Emmanuel_Macron" title="Emmanuel Macron">Emmanuel Macron</a> and <a href="/wiki/FIFA" title="FIFA">FIFA</a> president <a href="/wiki/Gianni_Infantino" title="Gianni Infantino">Gianni Infantino</a> at the <a href="/wiki/%C3%89lys%C3%A9e_Palace" title="Élysée Palace">Élysée Palace</a> in Paris that focused on a sports development project in Africa.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup> Mbappé stated that the development of African sport is important to him due to his parents' African origins.<sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;135&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 28 January 2019, Mbappé donated $34,000 (around £26,000) to a crowdfunding campaign to finance a private search mission to find football player <a href="/wiki/Emiliano_Sala" title="Emiliano Sala">Emiliano Sala</a>, whose light aircraft had <a href="/wiki/2019_Piper_PA-46_Malibu_crash" class="mw-redirect" title="2019 Piper PA-46 Malibu crash">gone missing</a> over the <a href="/wiki/English_Channel" title="English Channel">English Channel</a> a week earlier.<sup id="cite_ref-136" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-136">&#91;136&#93;</a></sup> Later, on 10 February 2019, Mbappé donated a further £27,000 to the GoFundMe campaign created to fund the search for the plane's still-missing pilot, David Ibbotson.<sup id="cite_ref-137" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-137">&#91;137&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
